nityagranthasthasya athaśandasya vivaraṇam   
  
athaśabdasya prasiddhiprakarṣasiddhanantarye saṃbhavati,   
arthāntaratātparyaparigraho'nupapanna iti bhāṣyādiṣu sthāpitam | atha gadyaiḥ   
[vakṣya ityādi ka kha ga ca jha] yathāvat prapattipratipādanānantaram tata   
eva tanniṣṭhādhikāriviśeṣasiddhisamanantaraṃ vā [vā śabdaḥ ka kha ga jha   
kośeṣu nāsti] |   
yathāvasthitasvarūparūpaguṇavibhūtilīlopakaraṇavistāramanusaṃdhāya tameva   
śaraṇamupagacchedakhiletyādinā iti vakṣyamāṇānusārācca atra   
tathāvidhaśaraṇāgativiṣayagadyagranthasya [viṣayagranthasya ka ca jha]   
pūrvavṛttatvaṃ vivakṣitamiti jñāyate | na ca tatra akhilajagadādhāra   
ityādivakṣyamāṇamātrapaṅktirvivakṣitā tasyāḥ prapattikaraṇatvādarśanāt   
yathāvasthitasvarūparūpaguṇavibhūtyādīnāṃ ca gadya eva prapañcanāt   
ananyaśaraṇastvatpādāravindayugalaṃ śaraṇamahaṃ prapadye iti ca tatra   
kaṇṭhokteḥ | tasmādyathokta evātra [atra iti padaṃ ka kha ga jha kośeṣu   
nāsti] athaśabdārthaḥ |  
  
paramaikāntiśabdārthaḥ  
  
paramaścāsau ekāntaśceti paramaikāntaḥ | so'syāstīti paramaikāntī | ekatra anto   
niścayaḥ prāpyatayā prāpakayā ca | tadubhayaṃ saṃbhūya paramaikāntaḥ |   
paramaścāsau ekāntī ca iti vā samāsaḥ |   
tatrāpyananyopāyatvānanyaprayojanatvayoḥ samuccayāt pāramyam |   
ananyopāyatvaṃ ca ananyadevatākatvaparyantam | yathoktam -  
  
caturvidhā mama janā bhaktā eva hi te śrutāḥ |  
teṣāmekāntinaḥ śreṣṭhāste caivānanyadevatāḥ ||  
  
iti | ananyaprayojanatvaṃ ca ātmānubhavānandanairapekṣyaparyantam | tadapyuktam   
-  
  
ye tu śiṣṭāstrayo bhaktāḥ phalakāmā hi te matāḥ |  
sarve cyavanadharmāṇaḥ pratibuddhastu mokṣabhāk ||  
  
iti | etena tulyanyāyatayā bhagavadanubhavānande'pi [etena bhagavadānande'pi   
ka kha ga jha] phalitvābhiprāyo nirastaḥ muktānandasyāpi   
sārvabhaumantaḥpuraśukakṣīrāsvādanasukhavat svatantreṇa pareṇaiva   
svaprītyarthamupapāditatvāt | evaṃvidhaṃ ca paramaikāntitvaṃ   
mantrasiddhāntādiniṣṭhe.vapi saṃbhavatīti pūrvādhikāre sdhāpitam | dṛśyate ca   
sadācāryasakāśāt yathāvasthitagadyatrayādiśrāviṇāmidānīmapi tatsaṃbhavaḥ |   
tatra hi yathāvat pārāvaryaniścayādanyabhavatyunmūlanena   
ananyadevatākatvādikaṃ ca [ca iti padaṃ gha kośeṣu na dṛśyate]   
sidhyati | tāṃ cāvasthāṃ svayamevāha bhagavān [āha ca svayameva bhagavān   
ka kha ga jha] -  
  
ananyadevatābhaktā ye madbhaktajanapriyāḥ |  
māmeva śaraṇaṃ prāptāste madbhaktāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||  
  
iti | niratiśayabhogyabhagavatsvarūpādiniścayena viṣayāntaravaimukhyāt   
ananyaprayojanatvamapi tatraiva sidhyati yasyāṃ daśāyāṃ bhagavānatyantāsanaḥ   
suhṛdādivat svacchandārāvanayogyo bhavati | yathoktaṃ bhagavatā śaunakena   
-  
  
parāṅmukhānāṃ govinde viṣayāsaktacetasām |  
teṣāṃ tatparamaṃ brahma dūrād dūratare sthitam ||  
  
tanmayatvena govinde ye narā nyastacetasaḥ |  
viṣayatyāginasteṣāṃ vijñeyaṃ ca tadantike ||  
  
iti |  
  
paramaikāntināṃ devatāntaravarjanam  
  
evaṃ parimitaviṣayatyāgināṃ parimitadevatāntaratyāgo niyamo bhavati  
  
kāṅkṣantaḥ karmaṇāṃ siddhiṃ yajanta iha devatāḥ |  
kṣipraṃ hi mānuṣe loke siddhirbhavati karmajā ||  
  
brahmāṇaṃ śitikaṇṭhaṃ ca yāścānyā devatāḥ smṛtāḥ |  
pratibuddha na sevante yasmāt parimitaṃ phalam ||  
  
iti parimitaphalasaṅgatadabhāvābhyāṃ [phalasaṅgasadasadbhāvābhyāṃ   
gha] devatāsaṃbandhāsaṃbandhapratipādanāt | ato yathā -  
  
paramātmani yo rakto virakto'paramātmani |  
sarveṣaṇāvinirmuktaḥ sa bhaikṣaṃ bhoktumarhati ||  
  
iti pratipāditasya paramātmetarasarvaviṣayaviraktasya pravrajitādhikāriṇo   
devatāntaravarjanam tathā triṣvapyāśramāntareṣu pratibuddhādhikāriṇaḥ |   
smaryate ca pravrajitānāṃ devatāntarārcanatyāgaḥ | atriḥ -  
  
traikālyamarcanaṃ viṣṇordevatānāṃ tadātmanām |  
namaskārārcanadīni kuryānnānyasya kasyacit ||  
  
iti | kratuḥ -  
  
īśvaro bhagavān viṣṇuḥ paramātmā mahānajaḥ |  
śāstā carācarasyaiko yatīnāṃ paramā gatiḥ ||  
  
iti | punaḥ sa evāha -  
  
dhyāyate'rcayate yo'nyaṃ viṣṇuliṅgamupāśritaḥ |  
kalpakoṭiśataiścāpi gatistasya na vidyate ||  
  
iti | evaṃ pratibuddhānāṃ sarveṣāṃ devatāntaravarjanaṃ prāgeva darśitam | etena   
-  
  
devatāpratimāṃ dṛṣṭvā yatiṃ caiva tridaṇḍinam |  
namaskāraṃ na kuryāccedupavāsena śudhyati ||  
  
ityādikamapi pratibuddhetaraviṣayaṃ mantavyam | pratibuddhasyāpi   
svanamaskārayogyabhagavattatparivārādipratimāsu labdhāvakāśametat |  
  
niṣiddhanuvartane samārādhanānarhatvam  
  
evaṃ paremaikāntiśabdenādhikāriviśeṣa uktaḥ | tasya ca  
  
paradārastaścaiva paradravyāpahārakaḥ |  
na spṛśenmāmanādṛtya spṛṣṭvā ca patito bhavet ||  
  
ityādibhiranarhatāpādakāni sarvāṇi [sarvāṇi ka kha ga ca jha kośeṣu   
nāsti] tatra tatra draṣṭavyāni | saṃgṛhītaṃ ca   
samārāthanopayuktasarvadravyasādhāraṇyena vaṅgivaṃśeśvaraiḥ -  
  
niṣedhāviṣayībhāvādṛte naivāparo guṇaḥ |  
prītiheduḥ pareśasya svārcanāṅgeṣu vastuṣu ||  
  
iti | ārādhakasyāpi hi arcanāṅgavastutvamaviśiṣṭam | yathā ca praśastajātiṣveva   
tulasyādipatrapadmādipuṣparambhādiphalagaṅgātoyādiṣu   
taistairupahatinimittairniṣedhaviṣayatā evamārādhake'pi yataḥ kutaścidupaghātādā   
prāyaścittādanarhatayā niṣedhaviṣayatvaṃ bhavati anyathā nāvirato duścaritāt   
ityādiśrutikopaprasaṅgāt upahativiṣayaspṛṣṭabimbādiṣu ca   
prāyaścittavidhānāt | brahmavido'pi hyuttarāghāśleṣavacanaṃ   
[prāmādikādiviṣayaṃ gha] prāmādikaviṣayamiti sthāpitaṃ bhāṣyādiṣu |   
sarvānnānumatiśca prāṇātyaye taddarśanāt ityādibhiśca sūtrairayamarthaḥ   
siddhaḥ | api ca rājavadupacāro hyatra vidhīyate |   
rājopacāravṛttiścāpacāraparihārapradhānā tadvadihāpi | yathā ca guṇavati   
rājani sevakānāṃ sāparādhānāmapi kṣāmaṇamātreṇa niraparādhatā tathehāpīti   
tallābhaḥ [iti lābhaḥ gha ṅ cha] | idamapi saṃgṛhītam -  
  
ajñānādathavā jñānādaparādheṣu satsvapi |  
prāpaścittaṃ kṣamasveti prārthanaikaiva kevalam ||  
  
iti | yattvanantramuktam -  
  
arcanādiṣvanarhatvānna kaścinnāparādhyati |  
ato'nanṅgikṛtāśeṣakartṛdoṣavimarśayā |  
kṛpayaivāsya devasya sarvo'pyarhati tatkriyām ||  
  
iti etadapi kṣāmaṇayogyatākhyāpakam anyathā kṣamasveti   
prārthanāvidhānānupapatteḥ [prārthanānupapatteḥ ka kha ga jha] | na   
caitāvatā kṛtāparādhena [kṛtāparādhena ka kha ga ca jha kośeṣu   
nāsti] nirbhayena bhavitavyam prakṣālanāddhi paṅkasya dūrādasparśanaṃ   
varam iti nyāyāt |  
  
akarmaṇyatāpādakā doṣāḥ   
  
atra cākarmaṇyatāhetūnaparādhānevamāha [aparādhānāha ka kha ga ca   
jha] bhagavān  
  
śṛṇu sundari tattvena āhārasya vinirṇayam |  
āhāro yastvanāhārastacchṛṇuṣva vas.umdhare ||  
  
bhojanaṃ yastu bhuñjīta mama yogāya mādhavi |  
aśubhaṃ karma kṛtvāpi puruṣo dharmasaṃśritaṃ ||  
  
āhāraṃ caiva karmaṇyamupayuñjīta nityaśaḥ |  
[sarve cātraiva karmaṇyā vrīhayaḥ śālayastathā | iti   
varāhapurāṇapāthaḥ] sarveṣāṃ ca tataḥ karma pravṛtteḥ prāṇadhāraṇam ||  
  
akarmaṇyāni vakṣyāmi yarina tuṣyāmi saṃprati |  
rājānnaṃ ca na bhoktavyaṃ mama bhaktaiḥ kadācana ||  
  
rājānnena tu bhuktena tvaparādho mahān bhavet |  
dvātriṃśadaparādhāṃstu na seveta mama priye ||  
  
bhojyānnapānāhāreṣu ye mayā parikīrtitāḥ |  
dandakāṣṭhamakhāditvā yastu māmupasarpati ||  
  
dvitīyamaparādhaṃ tu dharmavinna pravartate |  
gatvā maithunasaṅgaṃ tu yastu māṃ spṛśate naraḥ ||  
  
tṛtīyamaparādhaṃ tu kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
dṛṣṭvā tu mṛtakaṃ devi yastu māmupasarpati ||  
  
caturthamaparādhaṃ tu na kṣamāmi vasuṃdhare |  
spṛṣṭvā [dṛṣṭvā ka kha ga ca jha] rajasvalāṃ nārīṃ yastu   
māmupasarpati ||  
  
pañcamaṃ tvaparādhaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā vai na kṣamāmyaham |  
pṛṣṭvā tu mṛtakaṃ caiva saṃskāraṃ mṛtakasya vai ||  
  
aparādhamimaṃ ṣaṣthaṃ na kṣamāmi vasuṃdhare |  
mmārcanavidhau kāle vātaṃ muñcati nirghṛṇaḥ ||  
  
saptamaścāparādho'yaṃ mama devi na rocate |  
mamaivārcanakāle tu purīṣaṃ yastu muñcati ||  
  
aṣṭamaścāparādho'yaṃ mamātra tu na rocate |  
madīyārcanakāle tu yo hi vācā prabhāṣate ||  
  
navamaṃ cāparāthaṃ tu na kṣamāmi vasuṃdhare |  
yastu nīlena vastreṇa prāvṛto māṃ prapaśyati ||  
  
daśamaścāparādho'yaṃ mama devi na rocate |  
paridhāyaikavastraṃ ca yastu vai māṃ prapadyate [prapaśyati ka kha ga ca   
jha] ||  
  
ekādaśāparādhastu mama vipriyakāraṇam |  
kruddhastu yaśca karmāṇi kurute karmakārakaḥ ||  
  
dvādaśaṃ cāparādhaṃ tu kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
akarmaṇyapi puṣpāṇi yastu māmuṣakalpayet ||  
  
trayodaśāparādhaṃ tu na vakṣyāmi vasuṃdhare |  
yastu raktena vastreṇa kausumbhenādhigacchati ||  
  
caturdaśāpārādhaṃ tu na kṣamāmi vasuṃdhare |  
andhakāre tu māṃ devi yaḥ spṛśettu kadācana ||  
  
pañcadaśāparādhaṃ taṃ kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
yastu kṛṣṇena vastreṇa mama karmāṇi kārayet ||  
  
ṣoḍaśaṃ cāparādhaṃ taṃ kalpayāmi na saṃśayaḥ |  
vāsaḥ samavadhūnvan vai yastu mayyupakalpayet ||  
  
saptadaśāparādhaṃ taṃ kalpayāmi na saṃśayaḥ |  
vārāhaṃ yastu māṃsaṃ vai bhakṣayitvā prapadyate ||  
  
ekonaviṃśāparādhaṃ pratijānāti mādhavi |  
jālapādaṃ [jālaghātaṃ ka ṅ ca] samaśnan vai yastu māmupasarpati ||  
  
aparādhaṃ viṃśamimaṃ kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
spṛṣṭvā vai dīpakaṃ yastu mohāt spṛśati mādhavi ||  
  
ekaviṃśāparādhaṃ taṃ kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
śmaśānaṃ yastu vai gatvā mama caivābhigacchati ||  
  
dvāviṃśāparādhaṃ tu tamahaṃ copakalpaye |  
piṇyākaṃ bhakṣayitvā tu mama caivopasaṃkramet [ca kośādanyatra   
upacakramet iti pāthaḥ] ||  
  
trayovi.śāpārādhaṃ taṃ naro mama ca kalpayet |  
majjanānavajānan yo māṃ tu paśyati mādhavi ||  
  
caturviṃśāparādhaṃ taṃ kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
ekahastapraṇāmaṃ ca yaḥ karoti ca māmini ||  
  
pañcavi.śāparādhaṃ taṃ na kṣamāmi vasuṃdhare |  
paraprāpaṇakenaiva yastu māmabhigacchati ||  
  
saptaviṃśāparādhaṃ taṃ na kṣamāmi vasuṃdhare |  
navāgraṃ ye tu brīhīṇāmadattvāpīha bhuñjate ||  
  
aṣṭāviṃśāparādhaṃ taṃ kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
adattvā sumano yo vai dhūpaṃ me dātumicchati ||  
  
ekonatriṃśāparādhaṃ kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
lopānatkastu yo martyo māmevamupasarpati ||  
  
aparādhamimaṃ griṃśaṃ kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
bherīmatāḍayitvā tu yastu māṃ pratibodhati ||  
  
ekatriṃśāparādhaṃ tu kalpayāmi vasuṃdhare |  
ajīrṇarasamāviṣṭo yastu māmupasarpati |  
mahāparādhaṃ tadvidyād dvātriṃśamiha cottamam ||  
  
iti | evametānyanyāni cānarhatānimittāni pariharataḥ saṃbhave ca sānutāpaṃ   
yathocitaṃ prāyaścittamanutiṣṭhata iha samārādhanādhikāritvam |  
  
jātyādinibandhano'pyadhikāraviśeṣaḥ  
  
evaṃ jātyādinibandhanādhikāraviśeṣo'pi śāstreṣu śrūyate | yathoktaṃ   
śrīsāttvate -   
  
aṣṭāṅgayogasiddhānāṃ hṛdyāganiratātmanām |  
yogināmadhikāraḥ syādekasmin gṛdayeśaye ||  
  
vyāmiśrayāgamuktānāṃ viprāṇāṃ vedavedinām [vedavādinām kha ṅ   
cha] |  
samantre tu caturvyūhe tvadhikāro [mantre tu cāturvyūhe tu adhikāro ka kha ga   
ṅ ca jha] na cānyathā ||  
  
trayāṇāṃ kṣatriyādīnāṃ prapannānāṃ ca tattvataḥ |  
amantramadhikārastu cāturvyūhakriyākrame ||  
  
sakriye mantracakre tu vaibhavīye vivekinām |  
mamatāsaṃnirastānāṃ svakarmaniratātmanām ||  
  
karmavāṅmanasaiḥ samyagbhaktānāṃ parameśvare |  
caturṇāmadhikāro vai vṛtte [prāpte ka ca jha] dīkṣākrame sati ||  
  
evaṃ saṃpratipannānāṃ mantrapūrvaṃ yathāsthitam |  
vidhānamekamurtīyaṃ samānakarṇasya sāṃpratam ||  
  
iti | jayādiṣu cāptādibhedo draṣtvyaḥ | sarveṣāmantato bhagavatprāptiḥ samānā |   
vikalānāmapi bhāgavatānam* [*ṅap in all ṃṣṣ. and printed   
editions]  
  
iti ijyā   
svādhyāḥ   
  
atha svādyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | caturthe kāle saṃprāpte   
svāvagatavedavākyārthavyaktīkaraṇāya viditasakalavedatadarthānāṃ   
svayogamahimasākṣātkṛtaparāvaratattvayāthātmyānāṃ   
manuparāśarapārāśaryaśukaśaunakādīnāṃ maharṣīṇāṃ prabandhān   
[maharṣīṇāṃ prabandhān ityasya sthāne vedopabṛṃhaṇāni iti padaṃ kha ga   
ca jha kośeṣu dṛśyate] śravaṇamananajapādibhirabhyaset | tadidamuktaṃ   
vyāsena tatkālakṛtyam- itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛṃhayet iti |   
dakṣeṇa tu itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ saptamamabhyaset iti | evam   
bhuktvopastyāya cādityaṃ purāṇāni sadā paṭhet ityādikaṃ ca draṣṭavyam | jha   
kośeṣu dṛśyate] śravaṇamananajapādibhirabhyaset | tadidamuktaṃ vyāsena   
tatkālakṛtyam- itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛṃhayet iti | dakṣeṇa   
tu itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ saptamamabhyaset iti | evam bhuktvopastyāya   
cādityaṃ purāṇāni sadā paṭhet ityādikaṃ ca draṣṭavyam |   
upabṛṃhaṇanirapekṣasya upabṛṃhaṇīyavedabhāgajapa eva yuktaḥ | tatrāpi   
sākṣādbhagavatpratipādaka eva bhāgo japya iti śrīśāṇḍilyasmṛtyādiṣūktam |   
saṃgraharucīnāṃ mahāmantrasaktānāṃ ca   
sarvasārabhūtavyāpakamantrajapopadeśaḥ |  
  
japādikāle'pi gurvādiṣu maunavarjanaṃ sarvatroktam | āha caivaṃ codhāyanaḥ -  
  
स्वाध्यायमध्ये गुर्वादिपुरस्कारः   
  
जपमध्ये गुरुर्वापि वैष्णवो यः समागतः ।  
सम्भाषणादिपूजां तु तस्य कृत्वानुमान्य च ॥  
  
अनुश्राव्य ततः कुर्याज्जपशेषं समाहितः ।  
सर्वस्य प्रभवो यस्माद्विष्णुपादाश्रया नराः ॥  
तन्मूलतः क्रियाः सर्वाः सफलास्तु भवन्ति हि ॥  
  
इति । तत्र मौनमन्त्रार्थचिन्तनादयो नियमास्त्रत्र तत्र ग्राह्याः ।   
शिष्यगुरुसब्रह्मचारिभिः श्रेयोऽर्थिभिरनसूयुभिः वीतरागैः सह वादः   
बोधयन्तः प्रस्परम् इत्युक्तसंवादोऽपि तत्त्वनिर्णयफलत्वाविशेषात्   
इतिहासपुराणादिवत् स्वाध्यायकाल एव प्रवर्तनीयः । स्मरन्ति चाभिगमनान्तः   
पातिनि पूर्वयामस्वाध्याये जपेदध्यापयेच्छिप्यान् धारयेच्च विचारयेत् इति ।   
विचारोऽभ्यसनं जपः इति च [च कोशादन्यत्र चकारो न विद्यते] । उक्तं   
चानुयागविधानानन्तरं श्रीसात्त्वते समाचम्य पुनर्यात् प्रयतो   
भगवद्गृहम् इत्युक्त्वा  
  
मनोबुद्ध्यभिमानेन सह न्यस्य धरातले ।  
[कूर्मवदित्याद्युत्तरार्धं घ ङ् छ कोशेषु नास्ति] कूर्मवच्चतुरः   
पादान् शिरस्तत्रिव पञ्चनम् ॥  
  
इत्याष्टाङ्गप्रणामं[इत्यादिना साष्टाङ्गप्रणामं घ ङ् छ] च   
विधाय  
  
अष्टाङ्गेन नमस्कृत्य ह्युपविश्यात्रतो हरेः [विभोः घ ङ् छ] ।  
आगमाद्ययनं कुर्यात् तद्वाक्यार्थविचारणम् [विचारणात् ङ् छ] ॥  
  
इति । तदिह   
भगवत्प्रीणनस्वचित्तरञ्जकेतिहासपुराणस्तोत्रनिगमान्तद्वयव्यापकमन्त्रादी  
नां श्रवणमननप्रवचनजपादयो वादसंवादादयश्च   
यौगिकज्ञानप्रदीपस्नेहायमानाः   
  
पारुष्यमनृतं प्सिशुन्यं चैव सर्वशः ।  
अनिबद्धप्रलापश्च वाङ्मयं स्याच्चतुर्विधम् ॥  
  
इत्यादिनिदर्शितविविधवाचिकपापोदयप्रतिबन्धिनश्च सर्वे व्यापारा   
यथासम्भवं सम्भूय पृथग्भूय वा स्वाध्यायीभवन्ति ।   
शमाद्युपयुक्तशब्दशीलनं कुर्यादिति स्वाध्यायसारः । उक्तं हि   
महाभारते -  
  
यच्छृउतं न विरागाय न धर्माय न शान्तये ।  
सुबद्धमपि शब्देन काकवाशितमेव तत् ॥  
  
इति न शब्दशास्त्राभिरतस्य मोक्षः  इत्यादि च [इति च क ख ग च] ।  
  
सायंसन्ध्यादिकम्   
  
अथ लोहितायति भास्करे अथासूत्रं सायंसन्धोपासनं सायंहोमः   
पुनर्यथाशक्ति [भगवदभिगमनं क ख ग च झ]   
भगवदभिगमनहविर्निवेदनपूर्वकं भोजनम् । केनचिन्निमित्तेन विलुप्ते   
भोजने प्राणाग्निहोत्रमन्त्रजपः । ततश्च रात्रियोग्यस्वाध्यायो योगश्चेति   
क्रमः । तत्र प्रमाणानि -   
  
उभे सन्ध्ये भगवानभिगन्तव्यः   
  
नानिवेद्य हरेः किञ्चित् समश्नीआत्तु पावनम्   
  
सायं प्रातर्द्विजातीनामश्नं श्रुतिचोदितम् ।  
नान्तरा भोजनं कुर्यादग्निहोत्रसमो विधिः ॥  
  
प्राणाग्निहोत्रमन्त्रांश्च विलुप्ते भोजने जपेत्   
  
प्रदोषपश्चिमौ यामौ वेदाभ्यासेन यापयेत्   
  
तत्पूर्वापररात्रेषु युञ्जानः   
  
इत्यादीनि । [अनन्यप्रयोजनाधिकारिकर्तव्यपूर्वयाम् क अ झ]   
अनन्यप्रयोजनाधिकर्तव्यः पूर्वयामस्वाध्यायश्च त्रयोदश्यां   
प्रदोषाख्यकाले [कालांशे घ] वर्जनीयः । यथा सङ्गृहीतं   
कालविधाने-  
  
महाप्रदोषे मौनाचरणम्   
  
विषुवायनद्वितयपञ्चदशीप्रथमाष्टमीषु कलिनाथतिथौ ।  
रजनीमुखे च मदनाधिपतेर्विधिराह नाध्ययनकर्म नृणाम् ॥  
  
इति । स्मृत्यर्णए चैतदुपात्तम् -   
  
मितसन्ध्यस्त्रयोदश्यां संस्मर[त्रयोदश्यामस्मरन् क ख ग झ;   
त्रयोदश्यां च स्मरन् घ]न्नात्मनो हितम् ।  
अह्वोऽष्टांशेन संयुक्तं रात्र्यर्धं मौनमाचरेत् ॥  
  
इति ।  
  
एवं तत्कालनियतसावित्रीहोमादिव्यतिरिक्तदशायां प्रदोषाख्यकाले   
मौनविधानात् मन्त्रजपादिकमपि वर्जनीयम् । यथोक्तं कृष्णमन्त्रकल्पे -  
svādhyāyajapamātraṃ niṣidhyate | mantrajapādikaṃ tu vidhīyate | uktaṃ   
cāṣṭākṣarajapasya nityatvaṃ bodhāyanena -  
  
evaṃ guroḥ [guruḥ gha] samārabhya mantrānuṣṭhānamācaret |  
aṣṭākṣaraṃ japedvidvānnityamaṣṭasahasrakam ||  
  
ajaptvāsṭākṣaraṃ mantraṃ nāhamaśnāmi kiṃcana |  
yāvajjivaṃ japāmīti paścādaharaharjapet ||  
  
aṣṭākṣarajapo yasya nityo naimittiko'pi vā |  
kāmyo vāpi bhavet tasya nityā devārcanā [nityadevārcanā ka kha ca jha]   
smṛtā ||  
  
iti | na cātra maunavidhikāle bhagavddharmavicchedaḥ tadānīṃ yadhāvidhi   
maunānuṣṭhānasyaiva [yaghāvihitamaunānuṣṭhānasyaiva ka kha ṅ ca cha   
jha] bhagavatsevārūpatvāt | pravṛttiviṣayā nivṛttiviṣayā vā   
bhagavadājñaiva sarvadānuvartanīyetyacchidrānuṣṭhānasiddhiḥ | yadyapi ca   
atatkriyasya pradoṣe haridarśanādikaṃ pradiṣidhyate taccānupālitaṃ   
paramaikāntibhirbhāṣyakārādibhiḥ tathāpi [svagṛhārcāyāḥ   
ityatrasvaśabdaḥ gha ṅ cha kośeṣu na dṛśyate]   
svagṛhārcāyāstatkriyatvāttadanujñā [tatkriyatvāt iti bahuṣu kośeṣu   
pāṭhaḥ ka jha kośayoḥ paraṃ tatkriyātvāt iti vartate] | uktaṃ caivaṃ   
bodhāyanīye purāṇasārasamuccaye -   
  
āsthānasthaḥ sadā sevyo vimānasthastu kālataḥ |  
svagṛhe sarvadā sevyo madhyarātraṃ vinā prabhuḥ ||  
  
iti | madhyarātre'pyuparāgādinimittaviśeṣasaṃbhave   
snānādipūrvakabhagavatsevājapādikamavaśyakartavyatayā vidhīyata iti na   
virodhaḥ |  
  
svādhyāyayogayoḥ anuyāgāt pūrvameva samāhṛtyānuṣṭhānaṃ keṣāṃcinmate   
  
etau ca svādhyāyayogau ahnikānuyāgāt pūrvameva kuṣucit saṃhitāviśeṣeṣu   
samāhṛtyopadiśyate | yathā saṃgṛhītaṃ nārāyaṇamunibhiḥ =   
  
punaḥ praṇamya deveśamahno bhāge turīyake |  
dviṣaḍaṣṭaṣaḍaṇādimantreṣu svānusaṃhitam ||  
  
viśeṣeṇa japenmantramaṣṭottarasahasrakam |  
aṣṭottaraśataṃ vāpi yathāśakti daśāvaram  ||  
  
gurvādīṃśca namaskṛtya bījaśaktyādikaṃ tathā |  
mantranāthaṃ praṇamyeśamāpādādavalokayan [āpādādavalokayan   
ityārabhya svadhāma nītvā deveśaṃ iti yāvat kha ga kośayoḥ nāsti] ||  
  
japtvā ca suciraṃ yogamāsthāya praṇameddharim |  
svadhāma nītvā deveśaṃ [svadhā manasā deveśaṃ iti ka kośe] prahvaḥ   
saparivārakam ||  
  
tatrārghyādibhirabhyarcya rakṣāṃ kṛtvāstranāyakaiḥ |  
punaḥ punaḥ praṇamyātha homādyaṃ saṃvidhāya ca |  
anuyāgaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā kṛtakṛtyo bhavennaraḥ ||  
  
iti |  
  
ayameva kramo vistareṇoktastadgurubhirvaṅgivaṃśeśvaraiḥ | tathāhi -   
  
prāptamahnaścaturthāṃśaṃ svādhyāyārthamudīritam |  
vijñāpya viṣṇave tasmai labdhānujñastato'pi ca ||  
  
bāhyārthādakhilāccetaḥ smāhṛtyendriyaiḥ saha |  
japannasṭākṣaraṃ mantraṃ prāṇāyāmapuraḥsaram |  
prayataḥ parayā bhavatyā pūrvameva samāhitaḥ ||  
  
karāṅguliśarīreṣu nyāsān kṛtvā yathoditān |  
gurūn mantramṛṣiṃ chando devatāśca [ṛṣicchandodevatāśca cha]   
yathākramam ||  
  
śaktiṃ bījaṃ ca śirasā praṇamedevamādṛtaḥ [praṇameddevamāditaḥ ka   
jha; praṇamedevamāditaḥ kha ga] |  
idaṃ gurubhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ [pūrvebhyaḥ ka ca jha] kriyate śirasā namaḥ ||  
  
mantrajñānapradātṛbhyastadgurubhyo'pi sāṃpratam |  
namaste mantrarājāya namaste'sṭākṣarātmane ||  
  
namaste cetanādhāra parabhrahmābhidhāyine |  
sthitvāntarhṛdaye sarvānātmanaḥ saṃniyacchate ||  
  
ṛṣaye'ṣṭākṣarasyāntaryāmine haraye namaḥ |  
aṣṭākṣaramahāmantravarṇasaṃkhyābhimāninīm [saṃkhyābhidyāyinīm ka   
kha ṅ ca jha] ||  
  
chandaśca devīṃ gāyatrīṃ śirasā praṇamāmaham |  
mantraśaktiḥ sthitā yasminnāśriteṣṭārthadāyini [iṣṭārthasādhini kha ga;   
iṣṭārthadāyinī ca] ||  
  
padaṃ nārāyaṇāyeti śaktiṃ tāṃ praṇato'smyaham [praṇamāmyaham   
mudritakārikāpāṭhaḥ] |  
akārādutthitaṃ bījaṃ vāsudevābhivāyinaḥ [vāsudevabhidhayinam ṅ   
cha] ||  
  
tadbījamasya prabhavaṃ praṇavaṃ praṇato'smyaham |  
[mantrasya devatāṃ ityārabhya śirasā harim iti yāvat mantra śaktiḥ iti ślokāt   
pūrvaṃ ka kha ga ca jha kośeṣu paṭhyate] mantrasya devatāṃ āpi   
paramātmānamavyayam ||  
  
nārāyaṇaṃ paraṃ brahma nato'smi śirasā harim |  
praṇamya caivaṃ gurādīn gandhādyairabhipūjya ca ||  
  
aniśaṃ bhagavadbimbamāpīṭhādavalokayan [avalokayet ka kha ga ca jha] |  
japedaṣṭākṣaraṃ mantraṃ tadarthamanucintayan ||  
  
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ vā śataṃ vā daśa votsukaḥ |  
japānte manasā dhyātvā yathoktākṛtimacyutam ||  
  
saptnīkaṃ sanuyātraṃ sadvārapagaṇeśvaram |  
kṛtvaivaṃ manasā yogaṃ suciraṃ hṛṣṭamānasaḥ ||  
  
utthāya ca tato yogād daṇḍavat praṇipatya ca |  
stutvā ca bahubhiḥ stotraiḥ dṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇam ||  
  
stitvāgre devadevasya kṛtvā mūrdhniṃ svamañjalim [svama~jnalim   
ityanantaraṃ jitanta iti mantreṇa taṃ devaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajet iti mudritakārikāyāṃ   
ślokārdham adhikaṃ dṛśyate] |  
tataḥ svasmai prapannāya [tasmai prasannaya ka kha ga ṅ ca cha jha; svasmai   
prasannāya gha] datte tenābhaye sati ||  
  
nirbhayaḥ sarvabhūtebhyo bhavennirvṛtamānasaḥ |  
karmaṇyavasite tasmin turlabhe duṣkare'pi ca ||  
  
arghyaṃ dattvā yathāpurvaṃ svamātmānaṃ[svaṃ cātmānaṃ ka kha ga gha ṅ   
ca jha] nivedya ca |  
svanivedanamantreṇa dāsaśiṣyātmajātmanaḥ ||  
  
sādaraḥ svena [svodakaṃ svena ka kha ca jha; sodakaṃ svena ga ṅ cha]   
parātmane |  
nidadhyāt svaṃ ca kartṛtvaṃ tasminneva parātmani ||  
  
kṣāmayeccāparādhān svān jñānājñānopapāditān |  
asaṃkhyānaviṣahyāṃśca [asahyānaviṣahyāṃśca ka kha gha ca jha;   
asaṅkhyānapi saṃṅkhyāṃśca ga] kriyamāṇānaharniśam ||  
  
ajñānato'pyaśaktyā vāpyāyasyād duṣṭabhāvataḥ |  
kṛtāparādhaṃ kṛpayā kṣantumarhasi māṃ vibho ||  
  
ajñānādathavā jñānādaśubhaṃ yat kṛtaṃ mayā |  
kṣantavyaṃ tadaśeṣeṇa dāsyena ca gṛhāṇa mām ||  
  
upacārāpadeśena kṛtānaharaharmayā |  
apacārānimān sarvān kṣamasva puruṣottama ||  
  
śirasā prārthitenaivaṃ prasannena parātmanā |  
kṣāntasarvāpacāreṇa karuṇāmṛtavarṣiṇā ||  
  
vātsalyaudāryasauśīlyādyanantaguṇarāśinā [guṇaśālinā gha ṅ cha] ||  
  
aśaraṇyaśaraṇyena kṛpayā parayā svayā |  
sasmitālokamadhuramāhūyādbhutayā girā ||  
  
dattaṃ tatpadayoryugmaṃ svayameva svamūrdhani |  
vahaṃstaccaraṇasparśanihatāśeṣakalmaṣaḥ ||  
  
āsitvā suciraṃ tasya purataḥ parayā mudā |  
samutthāya tatastasmai bhūyo bhūyaḥ praṇamya ca ||  
  
smārayitvā svakaṃ dhāma tadyānāya praṇamya ca |  
dattvātha pādukāyugmaṃ tatra devaṃ samānayet [samāpayet gha ṅ cha]   
||  
  
saptnīkaṃ sānuyātraṃ sadvārapagaṇeśvaram |  
tatastadarhavinyāsaṃ sūpadhānaṃ svalaṃkṛtam ||  
  
anantabhogaśayanamadhirū.ghe parātmani |  
āsīnayostathā [tadā ka kha ga ca jha] devyordevapārśve yathāyatham ||  
  
āsīneṣu yathābhāgaṃ senānyādiṣu sarvataḥ |  
athārghyapādyācamanatāmbūlādi yathocitam ||  
  
devāya devīyuktāya sānugāya nivedya ca |  
praṇamya daṇḍavadbhūmyāṃ bhūyo bhūyaḥ puro hareḥ ||  
  
anuyāgādikaṃ cātha cikīrṣanāhnikaṃ vidhim |  
dattanujñaḥ pareṇāpi gamanāyātmano bahiḥ ||  
  
nirgandukāmo nikṣipya devaṃ dauvārikādiṣu |  
samayaḥ sanutāpaśca caṇḍādīna dārapālakān ||  
  
kumudādīn gaṇeśāṃśca cakrādīnyāyudhānyapi |  
garuḍaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa śeṣaṃ śeṣāśanaṃ tathā ||  
  
praṇamya smārayeddevaṃ sasnehādarasādhvasam [sādhvasaḥ ka kha ca   
jha] |  
nikṣipan jīvitamiva nyasyanniva mahānidhim ||  
  
nidhitsanniva cakṣuḥ svamarpayanniva kalpakam |  
sarve bhavantaḥ sagaṇāḥ saṃnaddhaḥ sarvadikṣvapi ||  
  
sāvadhānāśca tiṣṭhantu nikṣipāmi bhavatsvaham |  
mama nāthaṃ mama guruṃ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca me ||  
  
hariṃ śriyaṃ bhuvaṃ cāpi tān pālayata sarvataḥ |  
yathānikṣiptarūpaṃ me saṃdarśayata sarvadā ||  
  
bhavataḥ śaraṇaṃ gatvā vrajāmi gatasadvasaḥ |  
iti vijñāpya tān paścāt prārthayet hariṃ girā ||  
  
nanu deva tvamevaikaḥ sasthāvaracaraṃ jagat |  
brahmādisthāvarāntaṃ ca paripāsi bibharṣi ca ||  
  
saṃhariśyasi cāpyante rūpaiḥ svaiḥ svairyathepsitaiḥ |  
kena tvaṃ pālyase deva kena vā tvaṃ vihiṃsyase [vihanyase ka ca jha] ||  
  
atstvameva tvāṃ devayu canḍādīna pālakānapi |  
māṃ ca māmakamapyetat sarvaṃ gṛhamaśeṣataḥ ||  
  
pālayitvā svasaṃkalpamātreṇa madhusūdana |  
tvāṃ mayā tvayi nikṣiptaṃ viśvastenārthikalpaka ||  
  
āgatāya yathākālaṃ sarvaṃ me dātumarhasi |  
iti vijñāpya purato daṇḍavat praṇipatya ca ||  
  
homaṃ pitṛkriyāṃ paśādanuyāgādikaṃ ca yat |  
sarvamāvedya tenaiva niyuktastaccikīrṣayā ||  
  
vīkṣamāṇastamevaikaṃ cakṣuṣā snigdhapakṣmaṇā |  
murdhni nyastāñjalipuṭo viniṣkramya śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ||  
  
baddhvā kavāṭayugalaṃ rakṣāṃ kṛtvā praṇamya ca |  
homādyamanuyāgāntaṃ vaidhaṃ karma smācaret ||  
  
iti | evamaṣṭāṅgayajanamadhye svādhyāyayogayoḥ samāhṛtyopadeśāt   
tattaddeśakālāvasthābhedena yathākramānuṣṭhānāśaktau ijyāderapi   
yathocitakālāntare samāharaṇaṃ rahasyāmnāyādiṣu prapañcitamihāviruddhamiti   
sūcitam | svādhyāyayogayośca yathāvasaraṃ mātrayā sarvatrānupraveśaḥ   
prāgeva darśita iti vyākhyātaḥ svādhyāyaḥ |  
  
iti svādhyāyaḥ   
yogaḥ   
  
atha yogaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tatra ananyaprayojanādhikartavyo yogaviṣeṣaḥ   
īdṛśaḥ paramātmāyam ityādinā śrīśāṇḍilyasmṛtyuktaḥ prāgeva darśitaḥ |   
śrīsāttvatādyupadiṣṭayogaprakārāṇāmavirodhaśca samyak samarthitaḥ | tatra   
bhagavān parāśarastvevamāha [tatra parāśarastvevamāha bhagavān ka kha ga   
jha]-  
  
ātmaprayatnasāpekṣā viśiṣtā yā manogatiḥ |  
tasyā brahmaṇi saṃyogo yoga ityabhidhīyate ||  
  
iti | ayameva tvananyaprayojanasya yogaḥ | kṣudrayogāntarāṇi tu   
siddhyantarārthānyeva yogaśāstreṣu paṭhyante | yadyapi ananyaprayojanasyāpi tatra   
tatroktanyāsavidyābhedāt svaniṣṭhāviṣayatattatsaṃhitoktaprakriyābhedācca   
anusaṃdheyarūpaguṇavibhūtyādikaṃ nānā bhavati tathāpi   
svarūpanirūpakānandatvādipañcakanirūpitasvarūpai sarvaśeṣiṇi parasmina   
brahmaṇi śrīmati puruṣottame tattadvidyoditarūpādiviśeṣaviśiṣṭe   
manovṛttinairantaryarūpatvaṃ yogasyāviśiṣṭam | ata eva   
  
pṛthagbhūteṣu dṛṣṭeṣu caturṣvāśramakarmasu |  
samādhau yogamevaikaṃ śāṇḍilyaḥ samamuktavān ||  
  
iti mahābhāratavacanaṃ susaṃgataṃ [vacanamapi saṃgataṃ cha] bhavati |  
  
yoge anusaṃdheyā viṣayāḥ  
  
atra tu bhāṣyakārādyuktanityagadyastotrādiṣu yathānusaṃdhānamuktaṃ tathaiva   
tatsaṃpradāyaniṣṭhairanusaṃdheyam | śrīvaikuṇṭhagadye [tu śabdaḥ gha   
kośe'dhikaḥ paṭhyate] ananyagateḥ prapattimevāpavargopāyaṃ vidhāya   
tasyaiva kṣudhitasyārogasya kṣīrānnabhojanādivat [kṣīrānnabhojanavat ka kha   
ga ṅ ca jha] svayaṃprayojanatayaiva dhyānayogaviśeṣaḥ   
tadanubandhyanusaṃdhānaviśeṣāśca prapa"ñcitāḥ | tathahi   
svādhīnatrividhacetanācetanasvarūpasthitipravṛttibhedam ityārabhya svāmitvena   
suhṛttvena gurutvena ca parigṛhya ityantena   
prāpyaprāpakabhūtaśaraṇyādhyavasāyamuktvā anantaram   
eiāntikātyantikaparicaryaikamanorathaḥ iti puruṣārthaviśeṣalipsāyā   
ananyaprayojanatāṃ pratipādya tatprāptaye ca tatpādāmbujadvayaprapatteranyanna   
me kalpakoṭisahasreṇāpi sādhanamastīti manvānaḥ   
ityananyopāyatānusaṃdhānamabhidāya tasyaiva bhagavataḥ ityādinā   
mahāvibhūteḥ śrīmataḥ ityantena śaraṇyatvādyupayuktākārānabhidāya   
caraṇāravindayugalamananyātmasaṃjīvanena tadgatasarvabhāvena   
śaraṇamanuvrajet iti śaraṇavaraṇameva mokṣopāyatvena [mokṣopāyatvenāpi   
gha] vidhāya tataśca pratyahamātmjjīvanāyaivamanusmaret iti   
svatantraprapattiniṣṭhasyaiva pratyahaṃ [prāṇarakṣaṇārthaṃ iti   
ghakośādanyatra pāthaḥ] prāṇarakṣaṇārthabhojanādinyāyena   
ātmojjivanārthamanusmaraṇaviśeṣaṃ vidhāya vistareṇa prāpyāntargataṃ   
paramapadaṃ varṇayitvā mahati divyayogaparyaṅke'nantabhogini   
śrīmadvaiśvaryādidivyalokamātmakāntyā viśvamāpyāyayantyā   
śeṣaśeṣāśanādikaṃ sarvaṃ parijanaṃ   
bhagavatastattadavasthocitaparicaryāyāmājñāpayantyā   
śīlarūpaguṇavilāsādibhirātmānurūpayā śriyā sahāsīnam ityādinā bhagavantaṃ   
nārāyaṇaṃ dhyānayogena dṛṣṭvā ityantena paripurṇadhyānamuktvā punaḥ   
bhagavataḥ ityārabhya bhagavatparicaryāyāmāśāṃ vardhayitvā ityantena māṃ   
nayedyadi kākutsthastat tasya sadṛśaṃ bhavet kadā drakṣyati māṃ patiḥ itādivat   
puruṣārthaprāptimanorathaprakārān pratipādya tayaivāśayā   
tatprasādopabṛṃhitayā bhagavadabhigamanaṃ dūrāt saparivārasya bhagavato   
nārāyaṇasya samastaparivārāya ityādinā mantreṇapraṇamya utthāya punaḥ punaḥ   
praṇāmaṃ cābhidyāya [anantarameva ka jha]   
anantaramevamanusaṃdhānamuktam atyantasādhvasavinayāvanato bhūtvā   
bhagavarpārṣadagaṇanāyakairdvārapālakaiḥ kṛpayā snehagarbhayā   
dṛśāvalokitaḥ samyagabhivanditatastaistairevānumato bhagavantamupetya   
śrīmatā mūlamtreṇa māmaikāntikātyantikapricaryākaraṇāya parigṛhṇīpṣva iti   
yācamānaḥ praṇamya ātmānaṃ bhagavate nivedayet | tato bhagavatā   
amaryādaśīlavatā [amaryādāśīlavatā ka kha ga ca cha jha]   
atipremānvitenāvalokanena sarvadeśasarvakālasarvāvasthocitāntyaśeṣabhāvāya   
svīkṛto'nujñātaśca atyantasādhvasavinayāvanataḥ kiṃkurvāṇaḥ   
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhagavantaupāsīta | tataścānubhūyamānabhāvaviśeṣo   
niratiśayaprītyā anyat kiṃcit kartuṃ draṣṭuṃ smartumaśaktaḥ punarapi   
śeṣabhāvameva yācamāno   
bhagavantamevāvicchinnasrotorūpeṇāvalokanenāvalokayannasīta | tato bhagavatā   
svayamevātmasaṃjīvanenāvalokanenāvalokya sasmitamāhūya samastak.eśāpahaṃ   
niratiśayasukhhavahamātmīyaṃ śrīmatpādāravindayugalaṃ śirasi kṛtaṃ   
dhyātvā amṛtasāgarāntarimagnasarvāvayavaḥ sukhamāsīta iti |  
  
yoge gadyatrayasya pratyekamupayogaviśeṣaḥ   
  
api cātra dvayavyākhyānarūpe gadyatraye nirvedabhūyastayā   
kaiṃkaryatvarātiśayācca prābhātike'bhigamane mitagadyānusaṃdhānamucitam |   
bṛhadgadyaṃ tu samārādhanakāle viśeṣato'nusaṃdheyānāṃ   
svarūparūpaguṇavibhūtidevībhuṣaṇāyudhaparijanaparicchadadvārapālapārṣadādī  
nāṃ yathāvadanusaṃdhānahetutayā [anusaṃdheyatayā ka kha ga jha]   
yathavasthitasvarūparūpaguṇavibhūtililopakaraṇavistāramanusaṃdhāya tameva   
śaraṇamupagacchet akhiletyādinā iti samārādhanasyādau [samārādhanādau   
iti gha kośādanyatra pāṭhaḥ] ante ca bhāṣyakāraireva viniyuktam |   
śrīvaikuṇṭhagadyaṃ tu  
  
yāmunāryasudhāmbhodhimavagāhya yathāmati |  
ādāya bhaktiyogākhyaṃ ratnaṃ saṃdarśayāmyaham ||  
  
iti prārambhāt paścādapi dhyānayogena dṛṣṭvā ityabhidhānāt   
phalarūpavilakṣaṇānusaṃdhānabhedānāṃ vidhānāt   
avicchinnasrotorūpeṇāvalokanenāvalokayannasīta iti kaṇṭhokteśca yogārthakalpite   
kāle [yogārthasaṃkalpakāle ka kha ga ca jha] viśeṣato'nusaṃdheyamiti   
bhāṣyakārāśayaḥ pratīyate | na ca bhaktiyogākhyaṃ ratnam iti prārambhāt   
mupāyabhūtabhaktiviṣayo'yaṃ prabandha iti bhramitavyam ananyagatikasya   
prapatteravātropāyatvenopadeśāt; upāyabhūte phalabhūte cānusaṃdhānaviśeṣe   
bhaktiyogaśabdapravṛttyavirodhācca | tataḥ siddhopāyairapyayaṃ yogaḥ svakāle   
niveśanīyaḥ | yogakālāniyamādaikāgryānurūpai kālāntare'pi   
[anurūpakālāntare ka kha ga ca jha] kadācidbhavati | yāminyāṃ   
bhavaddhyānasya tu pāvanatvātiśayaḥ smaryate -   
  
prapannanāmapi yogānuṣṭhānasyam  
  
upapātakayukto'pi mahāpātakavānapi |  
yāminyāḥ pādamekaṃ tu brahmadhyānaṃ samācaret ||  
  
iti |  
  
yogasya pañcaprakārabhagavadrūpaviṣayatvam   
  
tataśca   
  
parasmin vyūhākhye vibhavanivahe'rcāvataraṇe   
[tathāpyantaryantaryajahat ka kha ga jha]   
tathāntaryantaryapyajahadadhikārādiniyamāḥ |  
nirudhya svaṃ cittaṃ niravadhimahānantajaladhau   
nirastānyāpekṣā nayata saphalaṃ kālamakhilam ||  
  
eṣu ca [cakāraḥ ka kha ga jha kiśeṣu nāsti] paravyūhaprabhṛtiṣu   
cittalambaneṣu prapattyekaniṣṭhā nāthamuniprabhutayaḥ sulabhatamatvena   
paripūrṇatvāviśeṣācca samāhitacitānāmapyanusaṃdheyamarcāvatārameva   
cetasaḥ śubhāśrayamālambanta | tatra yadyapi śīghrasākṣātkārahetubhūto   
mantraviśeṣa ucchinnasaṃpradāya iti vṛddhā vidāmāsuḥ tathāpi   
svāvagatairmantraviśeṣairamantrakaṃ vā yathāsaṃbhavaṃ yathāsaṃpradāyaṃ   
tadanusaṃdhānamasyāpyavarjanīyameva [tadanusaṃdhānamapyavarjanīyameva   
ka ṅ ca cha jha; tathānusaṃdhānamapyavarjanīyameva kha] | sarvātiśāyi   
ṣāḍguṇyaṃ saṃsthitaṃ mantrabimbayoḥ ityādinā tasya pūrṇatvaṃ siddham |   
śrīvaikhānase'pi tadanusaṃdhānasyaiva mukhyatvaṃ pratipāditam | yathoktaṃ   
kriyādhikāre mānasī homapūjā ca berapūjeti sā tridhā ityupakramya [iti   
prakramya gha ṅ cha]-   
  
yoge prapannasya arcāvatārānusaṃdhānaṃ mukhyam   
  
yathopayogaśakyatvāt kartuṃ puṣpādipūjanam |  
cakṣuṣaḥ prītikaraṇānmanaso'pi tathaiva ca [manaso hṛdayasya ca iti gha   
kośādanyatra pāṭhaḥ] ||  
  
prītyā saṃjāyate bhaktirbhaktasya sulabho hariḥ |  
tasmāt trayāṇāmeteṣāṃ berapūjā viśiṣyate ||  
  
iti | āha ca bhagavān śaunakaḥ  
  
surūpāṃ pratimāṃ viṣṇoḥ prasannavadanekṣaṇām |  
dṛtvātmanaḥ prītikarīṃ suvarṇarajatādibhiḥ ||  
  
tāmarcayet tāṃ praṇamet vā yajet tāṃ vicintayet |  
viśatyapāstadoṣastu tāmeva brahmarūpiṇīm ||  
  
iti | ato yatra dvacit bhagavadrūpe yathāśakti [yathāśakti ka kha ga jha kośeṣu   
nāsti; ataḥ dvacit bhagavadrūpanirantarānusaṃdhānaṃ kha]   
nirantarānusaṃdhānaṃ nādhamuniprabhṛtivat siddhopāyairapi nirveśanīyam   
[niveśanīyam ka kha ga jha] |  
  
evaṃ tu sāttvatokdaḥ saṃdhyādinidrāntakarmasaṃgrahaḥ -  
  
sāttvatādyuktaṃ sāyaṃsaṃdhyādikam   
  
prāpte'tha saṃdhyāsamaye snātvā vā jaghanāvadhi [snātvā ca jaghanāvadhi   
kha] |  
kṣālayitvā tataḥ kuryādvāsasāṃ parivartanam ||  
  
[arcayitvārdhyapūjādhaiḥ ka kha ga jha]   
arcayitvārghyapuṣpādyairdevamagniṃ yajettathā |  
yathāśakti japaṃ kuryādāsādya śayanaṃ tataḥ ||  
  
samādhāya bahirdevaṃ nirālambapade sthitam [sthitaḥ ṅ ca cha] |  
apramattena [aprayatnena ga gha ṅ cha] vai tāvadaniruddhena cetasā ||  
saha tenaiva vai nidrā yādavabhyeti sāṃpratam ||  
  
iti | pādme tvevamuktam-  
  
tataḥ paścimasaṃdhyāyāṃ prāptāyāṃ tatra coditam |  
japahomādikaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvā paramapuruṣam ||  
  
arcayitvā yathānyāyaṃ yathāpūrvamaśeṣataḥ |  
bhuktvā saṃviśya śayane samutthāya mahāniśi ||  
  
ācamya prayato bhūtvā dhyātvā paramapūruṣam |  
yogāsane samāsīno yuñjītātmānamātmani ||  
  
yathoktena prakāreṇa yathāśakti caturmukha |  
saṃhārakramamāśritya tattvānyātmani saṃharet ||  
  
ātmānaṃ cāpi hṛtpadme paramātmani viṣṭhite |  
saṃharedutthito yogāt svāpaṃ kleśāpahaṃ vrajet ||  
ityeṣa kathito brahman yogakālaśca pañcamaḥ ||  
  
yogasya yathāśaktyanuṣṭheyatvam   
  
iti | na caitannirantarabhagavadanusaṃdhānaṃ   
sanakādisādhyamasmadādibhirdu'śakamiti matvodāsitavyam yathārogyaṃ   
bhojanavat yathāśakti tadāsvādasyāparityājyatvāt | uktaṃ va [ca śabdo gha   
kośe nāsti] śrīmatprahlādena -  
  
āyāsaḥ smaraṇe ko'sya smṛto yacchati śobhanam |  
pāpakṣayaśca bhavati smaratāṃ tamaharniśam ||  
  
iti | ato yathā vā [vā śabdaḥ gha ṅ cha kośeṣu nāsti] -  
  
draṣṭumicchāmi te rūpamaiśvaraṃ parameśvara |  
manyase yadi tacchakyaṃ mayā draṣṭumiti prabho |  
yogeśvara tato me tvaṃ darśayātmānamavyayam ||  
  
bhagavatkaiṃkaryarūpanidrānubhavaprakāraḥ  
  
ityetāvadvādino'rjunasya bhagavān viśvarūpaṃ svātmānaṃ darśayāmāsa   
evamatrāpi svānubhavasāpekṣān [svānubhavatāpekṣāṇāṃ ṅ ca cha; gha   
kośo'tra śithilaḥ] yathāmanorathaṃ paramodāro bhagavāneva   
svātmānamanubhāvayati | ato niryatnalabdhena bhagavadanubhavānandasaṃdohena   
kṛtārtho'smīti manyamānaḥ karaṇakalebarānuguṇyāvadhi sukhamāsīno   
vividhavyāpārāyastasya [vyāpārāyattasya ka kha ṅ ca cha jha;   
vyāpārāyāsitasya ga] kariṣyamāṇayogopakaraṇabhūtasya karaṇavargasya   
viśrāntaye svayamupanamantīṃ nidrāṃ na nivārayet yuktasvapnāvabodhasya iti   
smaraṇāt | nidraiva tadā kaiṃkaryam | suṣuptau ca tadbhāvo nāḍīṣu   
tacchruterātmani ca iti śārīrakasutroktena prāsādakhaṭvāparyaṅkaynāyena   
[prāsādakhaṭvāṅgaparyaṅkanyāyena ga] nāḍīpurītadbrahmasu   
[brahmaṇi kha ga gha ṅ cha] svātmanaḥ śayanamanusaṃdhāya   
lakṣmīpariṣvaṅgavyañjakena mādhavaśabdena bhagavantaṃ saṃkīrtayan yathā   
priyayā saṃpariṣvaktaḥ ityārabhya prājñātmanā saṃpariṣvakto na bāhyaṃ   
kiṃcana veda nāntaram ityāmnātaprakriyayā [ityādiprakriyayā ka kha ga ca   
jha] [paramātmani parisvaṅga iti gha kośādanyatra pāṭhaḥ]   
paramātmapariṣvaṅgaviśeṣaṃ ca parāmṛśya yat karoṣi ityādiprasthānena   
nidrāmapi samārādhanatvena manyamānaḥ saṃśuddhaśuskapādaḥ   
śāstroktaprakāreṇa samucite sthāne śāstrīye śayanīye coditadikchirāḥ   
śuddhatvānagnatvādiniyamayuktaḥ [śuddhatvādiniyamayuktaḥ gha]   
śrīśāṇḍilyasmṛtyādyuktaprakāreṇa svārādhyasya   
bhagavataścaraṇāravindayorvinyastaśiraskaḥ śayanāsanayānādau ityādividhānāt   
tameva mādhavaṃ hṛdaye [hṛdaye'pi gha] dhyāyan tameva kīrtayan   
sukhaṃ śayīta | yadā yadā ca [ca śabdaḥ gha kośādanyatra nāsti]   
nidrāvicchedastadā tadā tameva dhyāyet | saṃkortayecca tāni nāmāni punarā   
nidrāgamāt | so'yaṃ pradoṣaprabhṛti brāhmamuhūrtāvadhi   
[muhūrtaparyantaṃ ṅ cha] sārasvatasrotasa [srota iva ka kha ca   
jha] iva viśramāntaritasya yogasyāvasaraḥ avasarāntare'pyaikāgryasaṃbhave   
karmāntarasaṃkocena svīkārya iti [svīkāryamiti kha ga gha ṅ cha]   
prāgevoktam ||  
  
iti yogaḥ  
  
pañcakālaparasya sarvo vyāpāraḥ kaiṃkaryarūpaḥ   
  
evaṃ vartamānasya sarvaḥ kālo'pyabandhyo bhavati sarve vyāpārāḥ   
kaiṃkaryarūpā bhavanti sarvo'pyānuṣaṅgiko bhogaḥ   
krīḍāśukakṣīrāsvādanyāyena svāmibhogaśeṣabhūto bhavatīti   
bhagavatkaiṃkaryakarateḥ   
paramaikāntino'nādimāyāniśāvasāne'nantamokṣāvasaraprāmbhe ca   
pratyuṣavadāsthito'yamāyuḥśeṣakāla iti | sa cāyamautsargikaḥ krama uktaḥ |   
apavāde tu vyutkramavilopādipravṛttiḥ | tathāhi-   
upavāsadivaseṣvekadaśyādiṣu anuyāgasya lopo bhavati | saptāṅgameva ca [ca   
kāraḥ ka ga ṅ ca jha kośeṣu nāsti] tadānīṃ yajanam |   
  
pañcakālānuṣṭhānakramasya kvacit apavādaḥ  
  
ata eva cānuyāgasyāniyatatvavyañjanāya bhāṣyakārāṇāṃ tadanuktiḥ |   
tadarthakālaśca [tadarthaḥ kālaśca gha ṅ cha] tasmin divase   
svādhyāyayogādiṣvanyatamena yathocitaṃ yāpanīyaḥ | kadācit dvādaśyādiṣu   
prabhāte pāraṇaṃ bhavati | tadarthaṃ pūrvaṃ yajane [pūrvayajane ka kha gha   
jha] kṛte'pi svakālaprāptaṃ madhyaṃdinayajanaṃ saptāṅgaṃ tiṣṭhati |   
vaiśeṣikārcaneṣu bahuṣu ekadivase kramāt saṃbhavastu aṅgaguṇavirodhe ca   
tādarthyāt iti nyāyena upādānādipravṛttirleśataḥ pratirudhyate | tatra   
pūrvadivasārjitairdravyaiḥ paropanītairvā tattatkriyāniṣpattiḥ | yajanaṃ ca sarvasmin   
kāle'bhyanujñātam | khinnavṛtteranyaparasyāturasya kalahādyupadrutasya ca   
bhojanāt pūrvaṃ yadākadācillabdhe'vasare [labdhāvasare ka kha ga ca jha]   
bhavati | atyantāśaktau tu ṛtvikputraśiṣyādibhiḥ svasamairanyaiḥ kāryate | tatra   
tvayamapavādaḥ samryate -   
  
vidhuro brahmacārī ca vānaprastho'tha bhiṣukaḥ |  
parārthaṃ karma kurvāṇāḥ pātayanti patanti ca ||  
  
iti | īṣacchaktau tu saṃkucitayajanam ekopacāramārabhya tattacchaktyātyanusāreṇa   
sahasropacārāntavidhānāt | viṣuvāyanadvitayapañcadaśī ityādinā   
pratiṣiddhe.vavasaresu vedābhyāsarūpasvādhyāyo lupyate | tadā   
tatkālamapyananyaparasya paradhānatamo yogaḥ samāskandanti |   
trayoda"īniśāmukhe ca tasyāpyapavādaṃ kecidichanti | tadāpi   
sarvakriyāntaranirodhapūrvakaṃ maunavratamanuṣṭhīyamānaṃ   
sāttvikatyāgaprakriyayā svakīyena mayā svaprītyarthaṃ bhagavataiva kāryate   
ityanusaṃdheyam | tasmāt āloḍya sarvaśāstrāṇi ityārabhya dheyo nārāyaṇaḥ   
sadā ityādibhiruktaṃ bhagavadanusmaraṇaṃ sarvatra sāvakāśam |   
avichinnasmṛtisaṃtatirūpatvādikaṃ tu mātrayā bhajyate |  
  
āśaucādiṣvapi bhagavatsaṃkīrtanādi kāryam   
  
evaṃ mṛtakasūtakādyaprāyatyakāleṣvapi   
prayatakartavyaśāstrīyasarvakarmavilopaḥ | tadānīṃ tu [vilopavattadānīṃ kha;   
vilopāttadānīṃ ga] maunāvasaravyatiriktaḥ kālaḥ saṃkīrtanena smaraṇena ca   
yāpanīyaḥ satataṃ kīrtayanto mām tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu māmanusmara   
ityādestadānīṃ nirapavādatvāt | pratyuta -  
  
cakrāyudhasya nāmāni sadā sarvatra kīrtayet |  
nāśaucaṃ kīrtanaṃ tasya pavitraṃ bhagavān hariḥ |  
nāśaucaṃ kīrtane tasya smaraṇe vāpi vidyate ||  
  
[apavitraḥ pavitro vā iti viṣṇudharme pāṭhaḥ] aśuciścāpyanācāraḥ   
sarvāvasthāṃ gato'pi [sarvāvasthāgato'pi gha ṅ cha] vā |  
yaḥ smaret puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ sa bāhyābhyantaraḥ śuciḥ ||  
  
ityādibhiḥ kīrtanasmaraṇayorāśaucakāle'pi anuṣṭheyatcokteḥ | kiṃca [kiṃca   
iti śabdo gha kośe nāsti]   
  
saṃkīrtayejjagannathaṃ vedaṃ vāpi samīrayet |  
dhyāyan kṛte yajan yajñaistretāyāṃ dvāpare'rcayan |  
yadāpnoti tadāpnoti kalau saṃkīrtya keśavam ||  
  
ityādibhiḥ deśakālāvasthādhikāryādyaviśeṣeṇa [adhikāryādiviśeṣeṇa   
gha; adhikāryādiviśeṣeṇa vihitavedābhyāsa kha ga; adhikāryādyaviśeṣeṇa   
vihitaṃ vedābhyāsa ka jha] vedābhyāsadhyānayajanārcanasthāne   
[dhyānajapārcanasthāne ka kha ga gha ca] tulyaphalatayā saṃkīrtanasya   
vihitatvāt prapannābhimatabhagavatprīteśca tāvataiva sulabhatvācca   
sarvadeśasarvakālādhikāryadyanuguṇaṃ saṃkīrtanameva karmāntaralopakāle   
samucitam | viśeṣataḥ kalidharmatvācca [kāladharmatvācca ka kha ga] |   
kalau yuge prayatasyāpi hyanyāśaktasya tadeva yuktam | yathāha bhagavān   
śaunakaḥ kīrtanādiva kṛṣṇasya muktabandhaḥ paraṃ vrajet iti | ata   
evābhigamanasya n kadācidapi lopaḥ aprayatasyāpi   
dūrāvasthitasya[dūrādavasthitasya gha ṅ cha]   
saṃkīrtanapraṇāmāñjalibandhabhāṣāstotralaukikavākyamātrapūrvakaprapadanaira  
pi tatsvarūpaniṣpatteḥ |  
  
nanu [bhāgavatasadācārya ka kha cha jha; bhāgavatasya gha] bhāgavatasya   
sadācāryasakāśāt samyagadhigatavedāntasya brahmavittvena   
sadyaḥśaucavidhānādanuvṛttaśaucāsiddheḥ kathaṃ karmavilopaḥ maivam   
rahasyāmnāyaniṣṭhānāmeva tacchākhāgṛhyoktaprakriyayā tadabhāvāt |   
mantrasiddhāntādiniṣṭhānāṃ tu dīkṣitānāmapi prakrāntamahotsavādhikāriṣveva   
tanniṣedhaḥ | yadyapi brahmavittvameteṣāmaviśiṣṭam [brahmavittvaṃ   
teṣāmapyaviśiṣṭaṃ ka kha ga ca jha; brahmavitvameva teṣāmaviśiṣṭaṃ ṅ   
cha] tathāpi kṛtādiṣu triṣu [triṣu śabdaḥ gha ca kośayoḥ nāsti]   
yugeṣu teṣāmapi sadyaḥśaucam vṛttasvādhyāyasaṃpannasyāvasaṃkocanaṃ   
tathā iti [ghaṭikā vyavasthā gha ṅ] vyavasthāvacanena kaliyuge   
vṛttadinimittaghasaṃkocapratiṣedhāt | na ca vācyam -  
  
ekāhācchudhyate vipro yo'gnivedasamanvitaḥ |  
vyahāt kevalavedastu nirguṇo daśabhirdinaiḥ ||  
  
ityādiṣuktasyāgnivedādinimittasyāghasaṃkocasyāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ na tu   
brahmavittvanimittasyeti [iti śabdaḥ gh ca kośayoḥ nāsti] | maivam   
yathoktabrahmavidāmapi vṛttaguṇaśabdena grahaṇasaṃbhave saṃkocakābhāvat |   
na ca brahmaviccabdena pravrajitagrahaṇaṃ  brahmavidāṃ pravrajitānāṃ ca   
sadyaḥśaucārhatvena [sadyaḥśaucānarhatvena gha ṅ cha]   
pṛthagupādānāt [pṛthugupādānāt | yathoktam ..... maivam |   
brahmavedanādīnāmapi ṅ cha; brahmavādināmapi gha; pṛthagupādānāditi   
yathoktabrahmavidāmapi ca atra kośāḥ pāṭhato bahudhā bhidyante | asmin sthale   
kha ga gha ṅ kośeṣu yathokta ityasyānantaraṃ maivamityasya pūrvaṃ ca   
paṅktilopasūcakāni cihnāni ca dṛśyate] | tarhi   
satrivratibrahmacāridātṛbrahmavidāṃ tathā iti sahapaṭhitānāṃ   
satriprabhṛtīnāmapi satravratabrahmacaryadānādiguṇa[guṇa iti padaṃ ka kha   
ga jha kośeṣu nāsti]nimittamaghasaṃkocanamiti teṣāmapetadantimayuge na   
syāditi cenna [na iti padaṃ ka kha ga ca jha kośeṣu nāsti]   
anuṣṭhānatastadvyavasthāpanāt | adyāpi hi sadyaḥ śaucaṃ vratyādiṣu   
śiṣṭairanuṣṭhīyate | na [śārīrādhigama iti gha kośādanyatra pāṭhaḥ]   
śārīrakādhigamasiddhabrahmavedanavatāmapi gṛhasthānāṃ kvacit   
tadhānuṣṭhānaṃ [tadanuṣṭhānaṃ ka kha ga ca jha] dṛśyate |   
anantabāhyakudṛṣṭisiddhantavyākulatattvādhyavasāye   
rāgādidoṣāndhakārabahule bahulaniśīthakhadyotakalpaguṇalave'pi [api   
śabdaḥ ka kha ga ca jha dośeṣu na dṛśyate] kaliviluptasvadharmavarge'smin   
kāle brahmavidāmasaṃbhavādeva [tadanuṣṭhānadarśanaṃ ka kha ga ṅ ca   
jha] tathānuṣṭhānādarśanamiti cet tarhi kasyedānīṃ brahmavidaḥ   
sadyaḥśaucena karmalopaṃ parijihīrṣasi   
  
kalau kṛtayugaṃ tasya kalistasya kṛte yuge |  
yasya cetasi govindo gṛdaye yasya nācyutaḥ ||  
  
iti nyāyena yaḥ kaścidyatra kvacid brahmavidathāpi [brhmavidapi ka kha ga ca   
jha] saṃbhavatīti cet satyam sa tāvat   
vyāsāgastyabṛgupativibhīṣaṇaprabhṛtibhistvayāpyadṛṣṭe kvacit pradeśe   
vartamānaḥ svāntarātmasākṣikaṃ tathānutiṣṭhatu nām tadanyeṣāṃ   
[anyeṣāṃ ka kha ga ca jha] tu bhāgavatamaryādāṃ praviṣṭānāṃ   
paripūrṇabrahmavittvābhāve'pi [hi śabdaḥ gha ṅ cha kośeṣu nāsti]   
hyupanītāvasthatvamātreṇa dvijatvavat [saṃskāraviśeṣādiyoga ka ṅ ca cha   
jha] saṃskāraveṣādiyogamātreṇa bhāgavatatvamātraṃ siddhamiti   
tāvanmātravaiśiṣṭya[vaiśiṣṭya gha kośādanyatra nāsti]śālināṃ   
tannibandhanādhasaṃkoce pramāṇaṃ kvacinna paśyāmaḥ | ata eva hi   
[hiśabdaḥ gha kośe nāsti] teṣāmapi pauṣkarādiṣu āśaucamanumatam |   
yattu tatratyasaṃskāraviśeṣavataḥ kasyacit āśauchakāle'pi   
mānasayāgamātramanumanyate tat   
gāyatrīsmaraṇapūrvakajalāñjaliprakṣepnyāyena netavyam | viṣṇvarcanamapi hi   
[hi śabdaḥ ka a jha kośeṣu nāsti] pratyakṣaśrutisiddhaṃ nityaṃ ceti   
prāgevoktam | mānasayāgamātrābhyanujñānena [mātrānujñānena ka a   
jha] śeṣaniṣedhaśca tatrāpi diddha iti |  
  
tadevaṃ svataḥ prāptimapavādaprakārāṃśca [apavādaprakāraṃ ca ka kha;   
prāptānapavādaprakārāṃśra ga; svataḥ prāpatamapavādaprakāraṃ ca ca]   
yathāvadadhigamyāyaṃ dharmo'nuṣṭheyaḥ |  
  
dharmānuṣṭhānaprakārasya durūhatvam   
  
ekaṃ yadi bhavecchāstraṃ jñānaṃ niḥsaṃśayaṃ bhavet |  
bahutvādiha śāstrāṇāṃ jñānatattvaṃ sudarlabham ||  
  
ityādibhiryāthārthyena   
ativitatagahanagambhīravividhavikalpabahutaraśāstrasaṃkṣobhajanitadiṅmohaśānt  
aye sarvaiḥ saṃkalanamātraṃ [śāntaye kalāmātraṃ ṅ ca cha; śāntaye   
sarvaiḥ saṃkalana iti paṅktiḥ gha kośe upanītāvatthatvamātreṇa iti   
pūrvanirdiṣṭavākyasyānantaraṃ pramādavaśāllikhitā pratibhāti]  tviha   
kṛtam | anenaiva prasthānena praśamitadiṅamohaiḥ samarthaiḥ ā pramātāt   
anuṣṭheyāni sarvāṇi karmāṇi pratyekaṃ   
bahutaretikartavyatāmukhyānukalpavikalpāpavādādividhāyakatattacchāstreṣu   
yathāvadadhigamyānuṣṭheyāni | hanta tarhi durjñāne duṣkare'smin prasthāne ko   
nām [adya iti śabdaḥ ka ga ca jha kośeṣu nāsti] adyādhikāri syāditi cet   
maivaṃ bhetavyam   
  
bhagavatpūjanasya nityatvasukaratvādikam   
  
na viṣṇvārādhanāt puṇyaṃ vidyate karma vaidikam |  
sarveṣāmeva dharmāṇāmuttamo vaiṣṇavo vidhiḥ ||  
  
nityaṃ viṣṇvarcanaṃ param ityādibhiḥ sarvottaratvena ca [ca śabdaḥ ka kha ga   
ca jha kośeṣu nāsti] nityatvena ca śrute'smin dharme aṣṭavarṣasya   
brahmacaryadharma iva yathākathaṃcidanupraveśasyāpi [api śabdaḥ ka kha ga   
ca jha kośeṣu nāsti] yuktatvāt   
  
svalpamapyasya dharmasya trāyate mahato bhayāt |  
na hi kalyāṇakṛt kaścid durgatiṃ tāt gacchati |  
jijñāsurapi yogasya śabdabrahmātivartate |  
  
ityādinyāyena [iti nyāyena ka kha ca jha] bhagavataivāśritavatsalena   
śeṣapūraṇāt | smaranti ca-   
  
sakṛduccaritaṃ [sakṛduccāritaṃ gha ṅ cha] yena   
harirityakṣaradvayam |  
baddhaḥ parikarastena mokṣāya gamanaṃ prati ||  
  
sāṃketyaṃ pārihāsyaṃ vā stobhaṃ helanameva vā |  
vaikuṇṭhanāmagrahaṇamaśeṣāghavināśanam ||  
  
sakṛt smṛto'i govindo nṛṇāṃ janmaśataiścitam |  
pāparāśiṃ dahatyāśu tūlarāśimivānalaḥ ||  
  
harirharati pāpāni duṣṭacittairapi smṛtaḥ |  
anicchayāpi saṃspṛṣṭo dahatyeva hi pāvakaḥ ||  
  
durgasaṃsārakāntāramapāramabhidhāvatām |  
ekaḥ kṛṣṇanamaskāro muktitīrasya deśikaḥ ||  
  
eko'pi kṛṣṇe sukṛtapraṇāmo daśāścamedhāvabhṛthena tulyaḥ |  
daśāśvamedhī punareti janma kṛṣṇapraṇāmī na punarbhavāya ||  
  
upoṣitaḥ poṣito vā dṛṣṭo vā [duṣṭo vā cha] praṇato'pi vā |  
prasahya harate pāpaṃ ko na seveddhariṃ tataḥ ||  
  
ko hi bhāro [ko'tibhāraḥ ka kha ga ṅ ca cha jha] harernāmni jihvāyāḥ   
[jihvayā ka kha jha] parikīrtane |  
  
āyāsaḥ smaraṇe ko'sya smṛto yacchati śobhanam |  
pāpakṣayaśca bhavati smaratāṃ tamaharniśam ||  
  
kiṃ tvayā nārcito devaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ |  
udakenāpyalābhe tu dravyāṇāṃ pūjitaḥ prabhuḥ ||  
  
anyat pūrṇādapāṃ kumbādanyat pādāvanejanāt |  
anyat kuśalasaṃpraśnānna cecchati janārdanaḥ ||  
  
patreṣu puṣpeṣu phaleṣu toyeṣvakrītalabhyeṣu sadaiva satsu |  
bhavatyekalabhye puruṣe purāṇe muktyai kimarthaṃ kriyate na yatnaḥ ||  
  
patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ toyaṃ yo me bhaktyā prayacchati |  
tadahaṃ bhakdyupahṛtamaśnāmi prayatātmanaḥ ||  
aṇvapyupahṛtaṃ bhaktairmama toṣāya [bhogāya kha ga gha] kalpate ||  
  
ityādi | uktaṃ ca nāradīye śrimataṣṭākṣarabrahmavidyāyāṃ   
ṣoḍaśopacāroktyanantaram-   
  
evvamaṣṭākṣareṇaiva sarvatrārcanakarmaṇi |  
upacārānimān kurvan bhaktiyuktena cetasā ||  
  
tulasīpadmapālāśasuvarṇakusumaiḥ śubhaiḥ |  
pūjayitvā jagannathaṃ phalamānantyamaśnute ||  
  
gandhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalairmūlaiḥ pagrairvāribhireva [phalaiḥ   
patrairdhūpairvāribhiḥ ka ca jha] vā |  
nityaṃ bhagavataḥ pūjāṃ yathāsaṃbhavamācaret ||  
  
samastalokanāthasya devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ |  
sākṣādbhagavato viṣṇoḥ pūjanaṃ janmanaḥ phalam ||  
  
iti | etena bhagavatpūjanasya nityatvaṃ sukaratvaṃ svayaṃprayojanatvaṃ ca   
vyaktamuktam |  
  
yat punaridaṃ vikalasamārāthanādau pratyavāyādikamucyate-   
  
nityārcane vaikalye'pi doṣābhāvaḥ   
  
sarpaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhyānaṃ yathā kāyaṃ [dṛṣṭvā naraḥ kāyaṃ kha ga ṅ   
cha; dṛṣṭvā mahākāvyaṃ gha] kampate ca muhurmuhuḥ |  
amantramarcakaṃ dṛṣṭvā tathā bhīto [mahābhītaḥ gha] janārdanaḥ ||  
  
gandhahīne bhayotpattiḥ puṣpahīne tu saṃkulam |  
naivedyahīne [nivedyahīne kha ga gha ṅ cha] durbhikṣaṃ maraṇaṃ   
mantrahīnake ||  
  
amantramavidhiṃ caivamakālaṃ caiva pūjanam |  
nityaṃ rāṣṭrabhayaṃ kuryāt tadgrāmaṃ [grāmastu iti cet sādhuḥ] tu   
vinaśyati ||  
  
amantraiṇaiva yatpūjyaṃ piśācāsuravarthnam |  
vyādhitaskaradoṣau ca annavṛṣṭirmahadbhayam ||  
  
ityādi tadetat sarvaṃ rājarāṣṭrādisamṛddhyartha[samṛddhyarthaṃ ka kha   
ga ca jha]kāmyārādhaneṣu anyeṣvapi pūrṇānuṣṭhānaśaktasya   
saṃpūrṇadravyasya lobhādibhistattaddhānau mukhyakalapsamarthasyānukalpena   
vṛttau ca [pravṛttau ca ka kha ga ca jha] doṣamāha na tu nitye karmaṇi   
[nityakarmaṇi ka ca jha] niṣkāmasya yathāśaktikaraṇe | smaranti ca   
manvādahaḥ -   
  
vedoditaṃ svakaṃ karma nityaṃ kuryādatandritaḥ |  
taddhi kurvan yathāśakti prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim ||  
  
ityādi | asti cānyo bhagavaddharmasya viśeṣaḥ yamadhikṛtyāyaṃ   
sāttvatasaṃgrahaḥ -   
  
sakṛt tryahaṃ ca saptāhaṃ pakṣaṃ māsamadhāpi vā |  
yo yajedvidhinānena bhaktiśraddhasamanvitaḥ ||  
  
so'pi yāyāt paraṃ sthānaṃ kiṃ punaryo'tra [yoga ka kha jha] saṃsthitaḥ |  
yāvajjīvāvadhiṃ kālaṃ baddhakakṣo mahāmatiḥ ||  
  
iti | etadeva saṃkṣiptaṃ nārāyaṇamunibhiḥ -   
  
dinamekamapi prīto yaḥ kuryānmadimānnaraḥ |  
sukṛtī kiṃ punaryāvajjivamevaṃ samācaret ||  
  
iti | uktaṃ cāhirbudhnyena -   
  
samārādhayastvevamekāhamapi nārada |  
muktiḥ kare sthitā [karasthitā ka kha ga ca jha] tasya sarve kāmāśca kiṃ   
punaḥ ||  
  
iti |  
  
tadidaṃ phalārthiviṣayam | anyeṣāṃ tu svayaṃprayojanatvaṃ prāgeva sthāpitam |   
tadabhiprāyeṇoktaṃ vaṅgivaṃśeśvaraiḥ -   
  
evamekadinaṃ vātha [yāvat ka kha ga ca jha] dvidinaṃ tridinaṃ tu vā |  
māsaṃ vā vatsaraṃ vāpi yāvajjīvitameva vā ||  
  
varteta bhaktyā parayā vaiṣṇavaḥ suciraṃ sukham |  
prārabdhe madhyato virghnairvicchinne'pyatra karmaṇi ||  
  
nānartho na ca naiṣphalyaṃ na kṛtāṃśasya saṃkṣayaḥ |  
prārabdheṣvasamāpteṣu vicchinnaṣvanyakarmasu ||  
  
bhavatyevaitadakhilaṃ vaidikeṣvitareṣvapi |  
kṛtaḥ svalpāṃśako'pyasya sthitvā suciramakṣayam ||  
  
trāyetaiva svakartāraṃ svaśaktyā bhavabhītitaḥ |  
śraddhāvānadhikāryasminnukte [yukte mudritakārikāpāṭhaḥ] karmaṇi   
vaiṣṇave ||  
  
nāparaḥ kulavṛttādiguṇaḥ karturviśeṣataḥ [kartuṃ viśeṣataḥ ka jha;   
kaścidviśeṣataḥ gha; kartṛviśeṣataḥ ca] |  
yena kenacideṣitrā bhāvyamasmiṃstu karmaṇi ||  
  
tasmin sudurlabhe labdhe [kriyaiva gha ṅ ca cha] kṛpaivānantarakriyā |  
jñānakramatapoyogayuktānapyadhikāriṇaḥ ||  
  
śraddhāhāniḥ paro doṣaścyāvayedadhikārataḥ |  
svoktāsūpaniṣatsvevamuktavānuttamaḥ pumān ||  
  
śraddhaśraddhe samuddiśya tasmācchraddha paro guṇaḥ |  
neha kālakriyākartṛdravyadigdeśasaṃśritā [saṃsthitā ka kha ga jha] ||  
  
eṣitāraṃ tadicchāṃ vā vihāyāsti niyantraṇā |  
niṣedhāviṣayībhāvādṛte naivāparo guṇaḥ ||  
  
prītihetuḥ pareśasya svārcanāṅgeṣu vastuṣu |  
ata evārcanāṅgāni dravyāṇi gaṇayan svayam ||  
  
prāha patrādimātrāṇi jātivarṇādibhirvinā |  
aho hariṃ bruvannevaṃ muktimetyapyaho aho ||  
  
aho aho sulabhatā kṛpā ceyamaho aho |  
astyeva nirmalaṃ toyamayatnasulabhaṃ bhuvi ||  
  
dṛśyante ca śubhā dūrvāḥ sulabhāḥ sarvadikṣvapi |  
asti jihvā hariṃ [vaktuṃ ṅ cha] stotumātmīyaivāsyamadhyagā ||  
  
svakarāvapi karmīṇau dhyātumastyeva mānasam |  
ato na hānirmantrāṇāṃ [yoga ṅ ca cha] yāgavighnakarī hareḥ ||  
  
sāmagryeṣā hi saṃpūrṇā [vaktrādiḥ mudritakārikāpāṭhaḥ]   
patrādyekaikameva tu |  
ajñānādathavā jñānādaparādheṣu satsvapi ||  
  
prāyaścittaṃ kṣamasveti prārthanaikaiva kevalam |  
satyasaṃkalpasaṃyukte sarvajñe sarvaśaktike ||  
  
nityanirdoṣaniḥsīmamahāvibhavayogini [mahāmahimayogini ṅ cha] |  
svādhīnatrividhāśeṣacidacidvastuśeṣiṇi ||  
  
nirmalānantvijñānanidhavudadhiśāyini |  
svasaṃkalpakṛtāśeṣajagajjanmalayasthitau ||  
  
arcanādiṣvanarhatvānna kaścinnāparādhyati |  
ato'naṅgikṛtāśeṣakartṛdoṣavimarśayā ||  
kṛpayaivāsya devasya sarvo'pyarhati tatrkriyām ||  
  
iti | atra tatkriyām iti sāmānyanirdeśāt yathādhikāraṃ sākṣāt samārādhanam   
paraistatpravartanam samārāvanāpekṣitapradānena śuśrūṣaṇam  ityādikaṃ   
sarvaṃ saṃgṛhītam | uktanyāyena ynūnādhikopacārādikamapi srvamupapāditaṃ   
mantavyam |  
  
api ca aprayatnalabhyairāntarapuṣpādibhirapi bhagavadupāsanaṃ smaryate -   
  
bhagavadārādhane āntarapuṣpādīnāṃ mukhyatvam   
  
ahiṃsā prathamaṃ puṣpaṃ puṣpamindriyanigrahaḥ |  
sarvabhūtadayā puṣpaṃ kṣamā puṣpaṃ viśeṣataḥ [tathaiva ca gha] ||  
  
jñānaṃ puṣpaṃ tapaḥ puṣpaṃ dyānaṃ puṣpaṃ tu saptamam |  
satyamevāsṭamaṃ puṣpaṃ tena tuṣyati deśavaḥ ||  
  
iti | āha ca bhagavān śaunakaḥ -   
  
rāgādyapetaṃ hṛdayaṃ vāgaduṣṭānṛtādinā |  
hiṃsādirahitaḥ kāyaḥ keśavārādhanaṃ trayam ||  
  
iti |  
  
pūrṇānuṣṭhatuḥ samāhṛtyānuṣṭhātuśca tulyaphalatvam   
  
pratyekaṃ saṃpūrṇasamārādhanamityarthaḥ | ato yathādhikāraṃ yathāśakyamatra   
śraddadhānaiḥ daryārdrahṛdayadeśikopadeśapūrvakamanupraviśya   
deśakāladaśādyānuguṇyenācchidraṃ yathākramaṃ samāhṛtya   
vānutiṣṭhadbhiḥ ananyaprayojanaiḥ paramaikāntibhiḥ   
anavadhikaparamapuruṣacaraṇaparicaraṇarūpam [paricaryārūpam ka kha ga ca   
jha] apavargaiścaryaṃ yathārogyaṃ yathāyogyaṃ cātraiva bhoitavyamiti   
siddham |  
  
granthopasaṃhāraḥ   
  
[savyaṃ pādaṃ prasārya śritaduritaharaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kuñjayitvā   
jānunyādhāya savyetarabhujamaparaṃ [savyetaramitarabhuja ka kha ga ṅ ca   
jha; savyetarabhujamitaraṃ ṅ cha] nāgabhoge nidhāya |  
paścādbhāhudvayena pratibhaṭaśamane [pradibhayaśamane gha]   
dhārayan śaṅkhacakre  
devībhūṣādijuṣṭo jayanatu [vitaratu ṅ cha] jagatāṃ śamaṃ   
vaikuṇṭhanāthaḥ [navajaladanibhaḥ pātu divyaḥ paro na - ityasminneva   
granthe ijyārambhe dṛśyamānaḥ pāṭhaḥ (137 puṭe)] ||   
viditanigamasīmnā veṅkaṭeśena tatta-  
dbahusamayasamakṣaṃ baddhajaitradhvajena |  
pratipadamavadhānaṃ puṣyatāṃ sāttvatānāṃ   
praṣadi vihiteyaṃ pañcakālasya rakṣā ||  
  
kaṇḍulāḥ [kila ca]kalikajjalāviladhiyaḥ kecijjaḍā niṣphalaṃ   
vikrośantu viyaccaraiḥ saha balivyatyāsavitrāsibhiḥ |  
moghāśāpi tathāvidheṣvavitatheṣvāryeṣvamoghā [ārgeṣvamoghā ka ca   
jha] bhṛ.śaṃ  
muktariśvaryamahāphalodgamadhiyā caryeyamācaryatām ||  
  
tyaktaṃ śāstramalepakaprabhṛtibhiḥ kiṃ tena tasyāgataṃ   
pradviṣṭaṃ jagadekacakṣuṣi divābhītaistatastasya kim |  
dugdhaṃ pittahatairjugupsitamatastasyāpi kiṃ durjanai-  
styaktaṃ cedapi matkṛtaṃ suruciraṃ kiṃ deśikaistyajyate ||  
  
iti śrīkavitārkikasiṃhasya sarvatantrasvatantrasya śrīmadveṅkaṭanāthasya  
vedāntācāryasya kṛtiṣu śrīpāñcarātrarakṣāyāṃ  
nityavyākhyānākhyaḥ   
  
tṛtīyo'dhikāraḥ   
  
śrīpāñcarātrarakṣāṃ saṃpūrṇā
